class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type=button class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Migrate to Spring Boot 3.0</h1></header>
<p><strong>org.openrewrite.java.spring.boot3.UpgradeSpringBoot_3_0</strong></p>
<p><em>Migrate applications to the latest Spring Boot 3.0 release. This recipe will modify an application's build files, make changes to deprecated/preferred APIs, and migrate configuration settings that have changes between versions. This recipe will also chain additional framework migrations (Spring Framework, Spring Data, etc) that are required as part of the migration to Spring Boot 2.7.</em></p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=tags>Tags<a href=#tags class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Tags" title="Direct link to Tags" translate=no></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class=""><a class="" href=/reference/recipes-by-tag#spring>spring</a></li>
<li class=""><a class="" href=/reference/recipes-by-tag#boot>boot</a></li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=recipe-source>Recipe source<a href=#recipe-source class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Recipe source" title="Direct link to Recipe source" translate=no></a></h2>
<p><a href=https://github.com/openrewrite/rewrite-spring/blob/main/src/main/resources/META-INF/rewrite/spring-boot-30.yml target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">GitHub: spring-boot-30.yml</a>,
<a href=https://github.com/openrewrite/rewrite-spring/issues target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Issue Tracker</a>,
<a href=https://central.sonatype.com/artifact/org.openrewrite.recipe/rewrite-spring/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Maven Central</a></p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"/></svg></span>info</div><div class=admonitionContent_BuS1><p>This recipe is composed of more than one recipe. If you want to customize the set of recipes this is composed of, you can find and copy the GitHub source for the recipe from the link above.</div></div>
<p>This recipe is available under the <a href=https://docs.moderne.io/licensing/moderne-source-available-license target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Moderne Source Available License</a>.</p>

<ul>

<li class="">addIfMissing: <code>false</code></li>
</ul>
</li>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=usage>Usage<a href=#usage class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Usage" title="Direct link to Usage" translate=no></a></h2>
<p>This recipe has no required configuration options. It can be activated by adding a dependency on <code>org.openrewrite.recipe:rewrite-spring</code> in your build file or by running a shell command (in which case no build changes are needed):</p>
<div class="theme-tabs-container tabs-container tabList__CuJ"><ul role=tablist aria-orientation=horizontal class=tabs><li role=tab tabindex=0 aria-selected=true class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP tabs__item--active">Gradle<li role=tab tabindex=-1 aria-selected=false class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP">Gradle init script<li role=tab tabindex=-1 aria-selected=false class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP">Maven POM<li role=tab tabindex=-1 aria-selected=false class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP">Maven Command Line<li role=tab tabindex=-1 aria-selected=false class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP">Moderne CLI</ul><div class=margin-top--md><div role=tabpanel class=tabItem_Ymn6><ol>

<li class="">Run <code>mvn rewrite:run</code> to run the recipe.</li>
</ol></div><div role=tabpanel class=tabItem_Ymn6 hidden><p>You will need to have <a href=https://maven.apache.org/download.cgi target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Maven</a> installed on your machine before you can run the following command.<div class="language-shell codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style=--prism-color:#9CDCFE;--prism-background-color:#1E1E1E><div class=codeBlockTitle_OeMC>shell</div><div class=codeBlockContent_QJqH><pre tabindex=0 class="prism-code language-shell codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style=color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E><code class=codeBlockLines_e6Vv><span class=token-line style=color:#9CDCFE><span class="token plain">mvn </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:rgb(156, 220, 254)">-U</span><span class="token plain"> org.openrewrite.maven:rewrite-maven-plugin:run </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:rgb(156, 220, 254)">-Drewrite.recipeArtifactCoordinates</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token plain">org.openrewrite.recipe:rewrite-spring:RELEASE </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:rgb(156, 220, 254)">-Drewrite.activeRecipes</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token plain">org.openrewrite.java.spring.boot3.UpgradeSpringBoot_3_0 </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:rgb(156, 220, 254)">-Drewrite.exportDatatables</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token plain">true</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div><div role=tabpanel class=tabItem_Ymn6 hidden><p>You will need to have configured the <a href=https://docs.moderne.io/user-documentation/moderne-cli/getting-started/cli-intro target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Moderne CLI</a> on your machine before you can run the following command.<div class="language-shell codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style=--prism-color:#9CDCFE;--prism-background-color:#1E1E1E><div class=codeBlockTitle_OeMC>shell</div><div class=codeBlockContent_QJqH><pre tabindex=0 class="prism-code language-shell codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style=color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E><code class=codeBlockLines_e6Vv><span class=token-line style=color:#9CDCFE><span class="token plain">mod run </span><span class="token builtin class-name" style="color:rgb(78, 201, 176)">.</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token parameter variable" style="color:rgb(156, 220, 254)">--recipe</span><span class="token plain"> UpgradeSpringBoot_3_0</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div><p>If the recipe is not available locally, then you can install it using:<div class="language-shell codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style=--prism-color:#9CDCFE;--prism-background-color:#1E1E1E><div class=codeBlockContent_QJqH><pre tabindex=0 class="prism-code language-shell codeBlock_bY9V thin-scrollbar" style=color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E><code class=codeBlockLines_e6Vv><span class=token-line style=color:#9CDCFE><span class="token plain">mod config recipes jar </span><span class="token function" style="color:rgb(220, 220, 170)">install</span><span class="token plain"> org.openrewrite.recipe:rewrite-spring:6.23.1</span><br/></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=see-how-this-recipe-works-across-multiple-open-source-repositories>See how this recipe works across multiple open-source repositories<a href=#see-how-this-recipe-works-across-multiple-open-source-repositories class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to See how this recipe works across multiple open-source repositories" title="Direct link to See how this recipe works across multiple open-source repositories" translate=no></a></h2>
<!-- -->
<div class=container_BFBG><div class=subContainer_WIBZ><p class=heading_koda>Run this recipe on OSS repos at scale with the Moderne SaaS.<div><a href=https://app.moderne.io/recipes/org.openrewrite.java.spring.boot3.UpgradeSpringBoot_3_0 target=_blank class=link_wr7g>Run this recipe here <svg xmlns=http://www.w3.org/2000/svg width=20 height=20 fill=none viewBox="0 0 20 20"><mask id=a width=20 height=20 x=0 y=0 maskUnits=userSpaceOnUse style=mask-type:alpha><path fill=#D9D9D9 d="M0 0h20v20H0z"/></mask><g mask=url(#a)><path fill=#FBFDFF d="M4.5 17q-.618 0-1.06-.44A1.45 1.45 0 0 1 3 15.5v-11q0-.618.44-1.06Q3.883 3 4.5 3H10v1.5H4.5v11h11V10H17v5.5q0 .619-.44 1.06-.44.44-1.06.44zm3.563-4L7 11.938 14.438 4.5H12V3h5v5h-1.5V5.563z"/></g></svg></a></div></div><div><div aria-owns=rmiz-modal- data-rmiz=""><div data-rmiz-content=not-found style=visibility:visible><img decoding=async loading=lazy src=/assets/images/run-at-scale-3760f923c92d80c68159db58a5930d85.png class=img_CujE /></div></div></div></div>
<p>The community edition of the Moderne platform enables you to easily run recipes across thousands of open-source repositories.</p>
<p>Please <a href=https://moderne.io/product target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">contact Moderne</a> for more information about safely running the recipes on your own codebase in a private SaaS.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=data-tables>Data Tables<a href=#data-tables class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Data Tables" title="Direct link to Data Tables" translate=no></a></h2>
<div class="theme-tabs-container tabs-container tabList__CuJ"><ul role=tablist aria-orientation=horizontal class=tabs><li role=tab tabindex=0 aria-selected=true class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP tabs__item--active">SourcesFileResults<li role=tab tabindex=-1 aria-selected=false class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP">SearchResults<li role=tab tabindex=-1 aria-selected=false class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP">SourcesFileErrors<li role=tab tabindex=-1 aria-selected=false class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP">RecipeRunStats<li role=tab tabindex=-1 aria-selected=false class="tabs__item tabItem_LNqP">MavenMetadataFailures</ul><div class=margin-top--md><div role=tabpanel class=tabItem_Ymn6><h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=source-files-that-had-results>Source files that had results<a href=#source-files-that-had-results class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Source files that had results" title="Direct link to Source files that had results" translate=no></a></h3><p><strong>org.openrewrite.table.SourcesFileResults</strong><p><em>Source files that were modified by the recipe run.</em><table><thead><tr><th>Column Name<th>Description<tbody><tr><td>Source path before the run<td>The source path of the file before the run. <code>null</code> when a source file was created during the run.<tr><td>Source path after the run<td>A recipe may modify the source path. This is the path after the run. <code>null</code> when a source file was deleted during the run.<tr><td>Parent of the recipe that made changes<td>In a hierarchical recipe, the parent of the recipe that made a change. Empty if this is the root of a hierarchy or if the recipe is not hierarchical at all.<tr><td>Recipe that made changes<td>The specific recipe that made a change.<tr><td>Estimated time saving<td>An estimated effort that a developer to fix manually instead of using this recipe, in unit of seconds.<tr><td>Cycle<td>The recipe cycle in which the change was made.</table></div><div role=tabpanel class=tabItem_Ymn6 hidden><h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=source-files-that-had-search-results>Source files that had search results<a href=#source-files-that-had-search-results class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Source files that had search results" title="Direct link to Source files that had search results" translate=no></a></h3><p><strong>org.openrewrite.table.SearchResults</strong><p><em>Search results that were found during the recipe run.</em><table><thead><tr><th>Column Name<th>Description<tbody><tr><td>Source path of search result before the run<td>The source path of the file with the search result markers present.<tr><td>Source path of search result after run the run<td>A recipe may modify the source path. This is the path after the run. <code>null</code> when a source file was deleted during the run.<tr><td>Result<td>The trimmed printed tree of the LST element that the marker is attached to.<tr><td>Description<td>The content of the description of the marker.<tr><td>Recipe that added the search marker<td>The specific recipe that added the Search marker.</table></div><div role=tabpanel class=tabItem_Ymn6 hidden><h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=source-files-that-errored-on-a-recipe>Source files that errored on a recipe<a href=#source-files-that-errored-on-a-recipe class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Source files that errored on a recipe" title="Direct link to Source files that errored on a recipe" translate=no></a></h3><p><strong>org.openrewrite.table.SourcesFileErrors</strong><p><em>The details of all errors produced by a recipe run.</em><table><thead><tr><th>Column Name<th>Description<tbody><tr><td>Source path<td>The file that failed to parse.<tr><td>Recipe that made changes<td>The specific recipe that made a change.<tr><td>Stack trace<td>The stack trace of the failure.</table></div><div role=tabpanel class=tabItem_Ymn6 hidden><h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=recipe-performance>Recipe performance<a href=#recipe-performance class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Recipe performance" title="Direct link to Recipe performance" translate=no></a></h3><p><strong>org.openrewrite.table.RecipeRunStats</strong><p><em>Statistics used in analyzing the performance of recipes.</em><table><thead><tr><th>Column Name<th>Description<tbody><tr><td>The recipe<td>The recipe whose stats are being measured both individually and cumulatively.<tr><td>Source file count<td>The number of source files the recipe ran over.<tr><td>Source file changed count<td>The number of source files which were changed in the recipe run. Includes files created, deleted, and edited.<tr><td>Cumulative scanning time (ns)<td>The total time spent across the scanning phase of this recipe.<tr><td>Max scanning time (ns)<td>The max time scanning any one source file.<tr><td>Cumulative edit time (ns)<td>The total time spent across the editing phase of this recipe.<tr><td>Max edit time (ns)<td>The max time editing any one source file.</table></div><div role=tabpanel class=tabItem_Ymn6 hidden><h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=maven-metadata-failures>Maven metadata failures<a href=#maven-metadata-failures class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Maven metadata failures" title="Direct link to Maven metadata failures" translate=no></a></h3><p><strong>org.openrewrite.maven.table.MavenMetadataFailures</strong><p><em>Attempts to resolve maven metadata that failed.</em><table><thead><tr><th>Column Name<th>Description<tbody><tr><td>Group id<td>The groupId of the artifact for which the metadata download failed.<tr><td>Artifact id<td>The artifactId of the artifact for which the metadata download failed.<tr><td>Version<td>The version of the artifact for which the metadata download failed.<tr><td>Maven repository<td>The URL of the Maven repository that the metadata download failed on.<tr><td>Snapshots<td>Does the repository support snapshots.<tr><td>Releases<td>Does the repository support releases.<tr><td>Failure<td>The reason the metadata download failed.</table></div></div></div></div><footer class="theme-doc-footer docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="row margin-top--sm theme-doc-footer-edit-meta-row"><div class="col noPrint_WFHX"><a
